ANALYSIS              HAUSER FESHBACH,                            2001900100063 
                      OPTICAL MODEL,                              2001900100064 
           .THE EXPERIMENTAL ELASTIC SCATTERING ARE COMPARED WITH 2001900100065 
            THE SUM OF THE CALCULATIONS OF COMPOUND ELASTIC AND   2001900100066 
            SHAPE-ELASTIC CONTRIBUTIONS.  THE FORMER IS CALCULATED2001900100067 
            WITH HAUSER-FESHBACH THEORY WITH LEVEL WIDTH          2001900100068 
            FLUCTUATION CORRECTIONS ACCORDING TO MOLDAUER.  THE   2001900100069 
            LATTER IS CALCULATED WITH THE OPTICAL MODEL AND EXCEPT2001900100070 
            FOR 73-TA-181 SPHERICAL POTENTIAL HAS BEEN USED.      2001900100071 
COMMENT    .ANGULAR DISTRIBUTIONS MEASURED IN THE ANGULAR REGION  2001900100072 
            20 DEG TO 160 DEG IN 10 DEG-STEP EXCEPT IN THE        2001900100073 
            FORWARD DIRECTIONS, WHERE MEASUREMENTS PERFORMED IN   2001900100074 
            5 DEG STEP.                                           2001900100075 
           .THE SIGNAL-TO-BACKGROUND RATIO AT THE POSITION OF THE 2001900100076 
            ELASTIC PEAK WAS 7 TO 1 IN THE MOST UNFAVOURABLE CASE 2001900100077 
            I.E. AT 8 MEV NEUTRON ENERGY AND AT THE FORWARD       2001900100078 
            SCATTERING ANGLES, BUT WAS MUCH MORE FAVOURABLE AT    2001900100079 
            LOWER ENERGIES.                                       2001900100080
